## 109. Aug 19, 2025 Â· 1:36 PM UTC Â· 1957798722668016032#m
- é“¾æŽ¥ï¼šhttps://twitter.com/19ys_GGboy/status/1957798722668016032#m
- ä½œè€…ï¼š@19ys_GGboy

> I'll make my case: I partially agree with @MikeyTrading here.
>  
> I'll start by saying our community would be obviously EXTREMELY happy to catch a bid from @theunipcs or @SolportTom (we already got it from @TheOnlyNom & @iruletrenches) â€” it definitely enhances trust in the token, improve visibility, volume and sets it up for future upside.
>  
> On the other hand, I strongly believe the belief that a BONK token only runs because Bonk Guy or Tom supports it is not the best narrative for the long term.
>  
> It'll create a situation where all tokens that are not catching bids from BONK core will eventually trend to zero â€” while the ones who do will leave their community with a "great, now what" feeling that sets expectations that could be too high to meet.
>  
> This means, catching bids from BONK could be perceived as the final goal for tokens in the ecosystem and eventually used for EL from frustrated holders in the short-medium term.
>  
> I propose a parallel initiative: bids are obviously welcome, but what if they're joined by:
>  
> 1. A BONK MM (trusted & transparent) that helps keeping the chart attractive by sustaining it in the long run;
>  
> 2. A DeFi roadmap, where token supported by BONK or "Bonk guys" are integrated into top protocols like Kamino, MarginFi, Marinade, Sanctum etc.
>  
> 3. Public support and updates from main channels, treating the Community Fund as a proper fund â€” periodically updating people on key metrics, key actions taken, highlights etc.
>  
> 4. (BONK is doing it already) CEX support, helping projects get listed on Tier 3-2-1 exchanges as they progress in MC, Holder count and Volume;
>  
> 5. Co-Marketing initiatives, with BONK facilitating visibility/publicity and reward campaigns for communities & new holders;
>  
> 6. Integration into the BONK Flywheel, with a small part of the buyback/burn fund dedicated to supported communities to help pay for their expenses, to distribute to the MM, to add to LP, to buyback/burn community tokens as well.
>  
> 7. Networking opportunities, including Pitch Days to their investors networks, brand advisory and more.
>  
> If all (or some) of these points are met, it will then definitely set a bright future for those community tokens supported by BONK as they became extremely attractive investments.
>  
> We cannot achieve the same results by just catching bids, I'm sure 99% of the people reading this will agree with me.
>  
> I'm interested to hear what @shax_btc, @19ys_GGboy, @Davidmeme2024 @0xd3bt and devs from @Hosico_on_sol @pomkori @BluechipDotSol @MonkeyGoodBoy etc. from the @bonk_fun eco think about this.
>  
> I'm sure it would be a great move and a win-win for everyone! BONK ON TOP ðŸ‘‘
